Author: Xi Yang <xi@terraindata.com>
Date:   Thu Jun 15 15:14:38 2017 +1000

    There is a null literal type shortcut for ESStructureClause, that when their fields in
    the def have the same name as the fields, a 'null' literal can be used to indicate that.
    
    This 'null' exception reduces the code readability, so we remove it.
    
    * For ESStructureClause in EQLSpec.ts that use 'null' type shortcut, change 'null' to the type that has the same name with the field.
    * Update the constructor of ESStructureClauses.ts

commit 74a0e3e002e30aeeeccb03aba4656e989e6df597
Author: Charles Tripp <charles@terraindata.com>
Date:   Mon Jun 5 16:06:23 2017 -0600

    + ESParser v0
    
    + ESParser v0 parses JSON into objects, producing several metadata outputs:
    + getTokens() : returns a list of ESParserToken objects representing, in order, each token & it's position in sthe
    source text, and what ESParserValueInfo it corresponds to
    + getValueInfos() : returns a list of ESParserValueInfo objects representing, in order, each value parsed and what
    ESParserToken's belong to that value
    + getErrors() : returns a list of ESParserError objects representing, in order, each error (if any) encountered while
    parsing the source text. Each error knows what token, and thus what value, it originated from.
    
    + Next steps include integrating this with the query route, moving it into the shared library, and enhancing it to
    detect and validate ES queries specifically.

commit 3246ade9d9f419aab962f6607b03d9c92e325967
Author: Xi Yang <xi@terraindata.com>
Date:   Mon Jun 5 22:39:57 2017 +1000

    + WIP: Make TF and Midway share QueryResponse, QueryRequest.
    + Make ResultManager aware of the shared code.
    + Add the QueryRequest to the QueryResponse.
    
    The code sharing is implemented in approach 4  C4: Don't include midway code to bundle.js,
    create a shared directory, put shared interfaces in the shared directory, then midway and
    TF implements the shared interface.).

commit f722e8756ffcc537efccd8a5f1eab43922566afc
Author: Xi Yang <xi@terraindata.com>
Date:   Mon Jun 5 13:32:03 2017 +1000

    + Make ResultManager aware of Midway's QueryResponse format in an approach that
      all midway code is included in webpack.js, and TF can access anycode in midway directly.
    
    As we discussed the design principle of code sharing in slack, we have 4 approaches:
    C1: Include midway code to bundle.js,  TF can directly import midway's code.
    C2: Include midway code to bundle.js, create a shared directory, then create or copy shared types that could access, implement or extend types from the midway in the shared directory. TF only access types in the shared directory
    C3: Don't include midway code to bundle.js, same as C2, but we have to also copy all types imported by the shared types in the type directory. This may lead to copying a lot of in-directly used types into the share directory.
    C4: Don't include midway code to bundle.js, create a shared directory, put shared interfaces in the shared directory, then midway and TF implements the shared interface.
    
    We decide to follow C4, so the next change will be in the C4 approach. We can compare and feel the pro/con of these two approaches.

commit 2d5369d685f8d88142e2e812ff29c1c62caba0b8
Author: Charles Tripp <charles@terraindata.com>
Date:   Fri May 19 15:45:41 2017 -0600

    + added JSON error reporting for ES when issuing invalid queries
    
    + ResultsManager modified so that ES queries are issued whenever the tql changes, and fixed bugs with not issuing
    queries when they should be
    
    + Using "clarinet" json parser to ensure proper line, column, and position for error messages
    
    + May return multiple parser errors, ordered by position within the query. Currently only the first error is reported
    because of restrictions in the legacy query API
    
    + Changed the query route API for ES slightly to allow a string to be passed instead of an object as the query body.
    This is intended to be used for detecting JSON errors, but may be used to pass an unparsed query string as well. The API
    spec allows and allows "any" type to be passed as the query body, so this change only affects the API when querying an
    ES database via the query route.

commit e6cba10d03add53ba6a6f9ab9101199b6e6c5e35
Author: Abhishek Kulkarni <abhishek.kulkarni@terraindata.com>
Date:   Fri May 19 13:56:47 2017 -0700

    Rewrite tasty.upsert().
    
    For upsert queries, tasty.query() will return a list of autogenerated IDs
    only for objects that don't have a primary key specified. tasty.upsert()
    returns creates a new array of objects from the ones upserted and maps
    the returned autogenerated IDs to the right objects.

commit 117fa85c69418fbcb0ef4d1012f58f17a4cce41f
Author: Abhishek Kulkarni <abhishek.kulkarni@terraindata.com>
Date:   Wed May 17 18:04:45 2017 -0700

    Fix elastic errors.
    
    + Avoid including `TastyTable` field in `ElasticQuery`.
      `ElasticQuery` is the type of objects returned by the elastic generator and it
      should be have a valid string representation. `TastyTable` maintains
      internal table state which is included when `ElasticQuery` is
      converted to a string. Instead of having backend-specific string
      generators, for now it's easier to include all the relevant
      information from a `TastyTable` as string members in the
      `ElasticQuery` object.
    + Tweak test cases to match the new `ElasticQuery` format.

commit a4ef776242e978339e5000d27a416082112c0dfe
Author: Charles Tripp <charles@terraindata.com>
Date:   Mon May 8 18:55:34 2017 -0600

    + Prepare for autoincremented primary keys to be returned
    
    + Made MySQLExecutor and SQLiteExecutor capable of executing several statements sequentially
    
    + Made SQLiteGenerator generate an array of statement strings instead of a single string
    
    + Made SQLiteGenerator generate multiple bulk REPLACE INTO VALUES statements based on what columns were defined in the
    given objects on an upsert
    
    + removed Tasty.execute()'s ability to consume a raw string (this capability shouldn't be exposed at this level as it is
    specific to only some databases)
    
    + bulk upsert is now delegated to the generator and executor instead of being handled within Tasty
    
    + TastyTable's state has been better hidden in a single member (___tastyTableState___ : TastyTableState)
    
    + TastyTable's interface has been improved slightly (see diff)
    
    + unit tests have all been adapted to match these changes

commit 16bff947abc080804b96dedfa7c0fe30376d9e82
Author: Charles Tripp <charles@terraindata.com>
Date:   Fri Apr 28 13:30:10 2017 -0600

    + refactored database-specific implementations each into their own directory
    
    + each database controller lives in /database/[databasename]
    + within the database controller directory are several files:
    + *Controller.ts : the controller for this database -- this is the central point of access for the database
    + *Config.ts : the configuration for this database -- this is what you pass to the controller when constructing it
    + /tasty/ : the subdirectory contraining the tasty executor and generator for this database
    + /client/ : the isomorpic wrapper around the underlying library -- provides univeral logging and access control
    
    + Tasty has been modified to work with the new structure. To use it make a controller and then call the getTasty()
    method.
    
    + the tests have been modified to use the new structure, and they have been moved to match the new directory structure

Merge: ada5f45a 9c211d05

Date:   Tue Jul 12 14:01:24 2016 -0700

    Merge branch 'tql-editor-action' into 'tql-editor'
    
    Adding a builder action for setVariantField
    
    Use this action like this:
    ```
    BuilderActions.setVariantField(this.props.algorithm.id, [field key], [value] );
    ```
    Example:
    ```
    BuilderActions.setVariantField(this.props.algorithm.id, 'mode', this.props.algorithm.mode === 'tql' ? 'cards' : 'tql');
    ```
    
    See merge request !10

    Merge branch 'authentication' into 'master'
    
    Authentication
    
    To test against Midway, clone http://git.terrain.int/terrain/midway and do `make`, which will run this branch and serve it out of Midway. You can then log in with any username and password "secret".
    
    When built in dev mode `npm start`, credentials aren't checked (anything works).
    
    See merge request !3
